# *there are* *now* <_num_> thousand *active attorneys* *in illinois*.
# *there are* *now* <more than _high_> thousand *active attorneys* *in illinois*.
# contradiction
# *there are*: there are; we employ; the average is; re-testing applies to; 
# *now*: now; many; certainly; no; 
# *active attorneys*: active attorneys; duplexes; stray dogs; fast food restaurants; 
# *in illinois*: in illinois; practicing criminal law; on the list; in current litigation;

there are now 129 thousand active attorneys practicing criminal law.
there are now more than 179 thousand active attorneys practicing criminal law.
contradiction

# args:  <<*there are* = there are>>  <<*now* = now>>  <<*active attorneys* = duplexes>>  <<*in illinois* = practicing criminal law>>

### Hypothesis: 2
# *there are* *now* <_num_> thousand *active attorneys* *in illinois*.
# *there are* *now* <more than _num_> thousand *active attorneys* *in illinois*.
# contradiction
# *there are*: there are; we employ; the average is; re-testing applies to; 
# *now*: now; many; certainly; no; 
# *active attorneys*: active attorneys; duplexes; stray dogs; fast food restaurants; 
# *in illinois*: in illinois; practicing criminal law; on the list; in current litigation; 

# args:  <<*there are* = there are>>  <<*now* = now>>  <<*active attorneys* = active attorneys>>  <<*in illinois* = in illinois>> 
there are now 170 thousand active attorneys in illinois.
there are now more than 170 thousand active attorneys in illinois.
contradiction

# args:  <<*there are* = there are>>  <<*now* = now>>  <<*active attorneys* = active attorneys>>  <<*in illinois* = practicing criminal law>> 
there are now 177 thousand active attorneys practicing criminal law.
there are now more than 177 thousand active attorneys practicing criminal law.
contradiction

# args:  <<*there are* = there are>>  <<*now* = now>>  <<*active attorneys* = active attorneys>>  <<*in illinois* = on the list>>

contradiction
